
Test configuration : Firefox <--SOCKS V5--> JS OP (outside of the browser for now)

Target url : http://www.lepoint.fr/science

URL Encryption : for these tests the encryption algorithm just consists in reverting the order of characters :
	http://www.lepoint.fr/high-tech-internet --> http://rf.tniopel.www.com/high-tech-internet/
	http://www.facebook.com --> http://rf.tniopel.www.com/moc.koobecaf.www//:ptth
	
	For the tests http is used but later :
	
	http://www.lepoint.fr/high-tech-internet --> https://rf.tniopel.www.com/high-tech-internet/
	http://www.facebook.com --> https://rf.tniopel.www.com/moc.koobecaf.www//:ptth
	
	Note when the domain is the target one, the second part of the url is not encrypted, TBD if it is needed or not since it will be TLS encrypted
	
Process : the OP does load the real pages from the fake urls received and modify the request and response headers when needed so it can master what needs to be changed in the page (transformation of urls) and add a script to "tame" the result page (ie to control scripts, iframes, objects ... potential further insertions)

Results : 
	Most of the urls are correctly loaded, css files are not filtered for now so we can still see in the log some urls going to the real domain (www.lepoint.fr)
	Some urls can be broken (kcilcelbuod --> doubleclick) because they are inserted via document.write that the parser does not handle for now
	
Performances :
	Not optimized for now (logs, circuits creation time, process) but acceptable.
	
Logs : see below, FF logs and OP logs
